#ifdef VERTEX

attribute highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = (-_LightPow) + _LightOffset;
    u_xlat0.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat6.x = max(u_xlat6.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat6.x);
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat6.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + (-_LightPow);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat0.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat2.xxx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat3.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat6.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = u_xlat2.z * u_xlat0.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.w = in_POSITION0.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_5.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_5.y;
    u_xlat16_1.w = u_xlat16_5.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_1;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat2.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat2.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_7 = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_1.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_7)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_1.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_1.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_1.z;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat6.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat6.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;

uniform 	vec4 _DarkColor;
uniform 	vec4 _DownColor;
uniform 	vec4 _RimColor;
uniform 	float _HighBlend;
uniform 	float _HighOffset;
uniform 	float _HighColor;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[4];
uniform 	mediump float _Cutoff;
uniform 	mediump float _NormalStrong;
uniform 	mediump float _CustomAlpha;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _ExposureColor;
uniform lowp sampler2D _MainTex;
uniform lowp sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
uniform lowp sampler2D _RampMap;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
#define SV_Target0 gl_FragData[0]
vec3 u_xlat0;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
lowp vec3 u_xlat10_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
lowp vec3 u_xlat10_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat18;
bool u_xlatb18;
void main()
{
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat10_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
    u_xlatb18 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
    if(u_xlatb18){discard;}
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = (-_DarkColor.xyz) + _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD3.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz + _DarkColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _DownColor.xyz + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(vec3(_HighColor, _HighColor, _HighColor)) * u_xlat2.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + (-_DownColor.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD0.w + _HighOffset;
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat18 = log2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * _HighBlend;
    u_xlat18 = exp2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz + _DownColor.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD0.zzz * _RimColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat10_3.xyz = texture2D(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat10_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalStrong, _NormalStrong));
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-vs_TEXCOORD2.zxy) + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat3.yzx * (-vs_TEXCOORD2.zxy);
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.yzx) * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat10_2.xyz = texture2D(_RampMap, u_xlat16_1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD3.w * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat10_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat18) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz / u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    SV_Target0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    SV_Target0.w = _CustomAlpha;
    return;
}

#else

#else

    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat2.xxx;

    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_1;

    u_xlat2.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat2.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;

    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_1.z;

    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat6.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat6.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat3.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat3.xxxx + u_xlat0;

UNITY_BINDING(0) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;

vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat18;
bool u_xlatb18;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb18 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb18 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb18){discard;}
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = (-_DarkColor.xyz) + _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD3.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz + _DarkColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _DownColor.xyz + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(vec3(_HighColor, _HighColor, _HighColor)) * u_xlat2.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + (-_DownColor.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD0.w + _HighOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18 = log2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * _HighBlend;
    u_xlat18 = exp2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz + _DownColor.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD0.zzz * _RimColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalStrong, _NormalStrong));
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-vs_TEXCOORD2.zxy) + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat3.yzx * (-vs_TEXCOORD2.zxy);
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.yzx) * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_RampMap, u_xlat16_1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD3.w * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat18) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz + (-unity_FogColor.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD11.www * u_xlat16_1.xyz + unity_FogColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz / u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    SV_Target0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    SV_Target0.w = _CustomAlpha;
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_3.z = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-vs_TEXCOORD2.zxy) + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat4.yzx * (-vs_TEXCOORD2.zxy);
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.yzx) * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat10_2.xyz = texture2D(_RampMap, u_xlat16_1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD3.w * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat10_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat18) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz / u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    SV_Target0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    SV_Target0.w = _CustomAlpha;
    return;

{

    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb18 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb18 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;

    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD0.w + _HighOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * _HighBlend;
    u_xlat18 = exp2(u_xlat18);

    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;

    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalStrong, _NormalStrong));
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_3.y = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_3.z = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);

void main()
{

    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_7 = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_1.x;

    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_1.z;

    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat6.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat6.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat3.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat3.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;

mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;

mediump float u_xlat16_19;

void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalStrong, _NormalStrong));
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-vs_TEXCOORD2.zxy) + (-u_xlat3.xyz);

    u_xlat20 = inversesqrt(u_xlat20);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat20) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat3.yzx * (-vs_TEXCOORD2.zxy);
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.yzx) * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = inversesqrt(u_xlat20);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat20) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_RampMap, u_xlat16_1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat3.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat3.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat3.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_0.w * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat0.xyz = (-_DarkColor.xyz) + _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD3.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz + _DarkColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _SSSColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = _DownColor.xyz + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(vec3(_HighColor, _HighColor, _HighColor)) * u_xlat3.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + (-_DownColor.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD0.w + _HighOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18 = log2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * _HighBlend;
    u_xlat18 = exp2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz + _DownColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD0.zzz * _RimColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD3.w * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat18) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_19) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz / u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    SV_Target0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    SV_Target0.w = _CustomAlpha;
    return;
}

    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-vs_TEXCOORD2.zxy) + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = inversesqrt(u_xlat20);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat20) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat3.yzx * (-vs_TEXCOORD2.zxy);
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.yzx) * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = inversesqrt(u_xlat20);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat20) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat10_2.xyz = texture2D(_RampMap, u_xlat16_1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat3.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat3.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat3.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat10_0.w * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat0.xyz = (-_DarkColor.xyz) + _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD3.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz + _DarkColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _SSSColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = _DownColor.xyz + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(vec3(_HighColor, _HighColor, _HighColor)) * u_xlat3.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + (-_DownColor.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD0.w + _HighOffset;
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat18 = log2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * _HighBlend;
    u_xlat18 = exp2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz + _DownColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD0.zzz * _RimColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD3.w * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat10_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat18) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_19) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + (-unity_FogColor.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD11.www * u_xlat16_1.xyz + unity_FogColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz / u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    SV_Target0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    SV_Target0.w = _CustomAlpha;
    return;
}

    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;

#endif

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cutoff;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _NormalStrong;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RenderType;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cull;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ZWrite;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ZTest;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AlphaToMask;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DstBlendFactor;

};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD10;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
mediump float u_xlat16_7;
float u_xlat18;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = (-_LightPow) + _LightOffset;
    u_xlat0.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat6.x = max(u_xlat6.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat6.x);
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat6.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + (-_LightPow);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat2.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat0.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat2.xxx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat3.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat6.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = u_xlat2.z * u_xlat0.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.w = in_POSITION0.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * unity_LightmapST.xy + unity_LightmapST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_5.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_5.y;
    u_xlat16_1.w = u_xlat16_5.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_1;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat2.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat2.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_7 = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_1.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_7)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_1.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_1.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_1.z;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat6.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat6.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat3.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat3.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D unity_Lightmap;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
bool u_xlatb2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_19;
float u_xlat20;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalStrong, _NormalStrong));
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-vs_TEXCOORD2.zxy) + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = inversesqrt(u_xlat20);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat20) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat3.yzx * (-vs_TEXCOORD2.zxy);
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.yzx) * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = inversesqrt(u_xlat20);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat20) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_RampMap, u_xlat16_1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(unity_Lightmap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy).wxyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yzw * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);
    u_xlat20 = max(u_xlat16_3.x, _MaxShadow);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat3.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat3.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat3.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat20) * u_xlat3.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_0.w * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat0.xyz = (-_DarkColor.xyz) + _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD3.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz + _DarkColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _SSSColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = _DownColor.xyz + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(vec3(_HighColor, _HighColor, _HighColor)) * u_xlat3.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + (-_DownColor.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD0.w + _HighOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18 = log2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * _HighBlend;
    u_xlat18 = exp2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz + _DownColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD0.zzz * _RimColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD3.w * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat18) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_19) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz / u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    SV_Target0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    SV_Target0.w = _CustomAlpha;
    return;
}

"// hash: f96d64b90d7c2443

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = (-_LightPow) + _LightOffset;
    u_xlat0.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat6.x = max(u_xlat6.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat6.x);
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat6.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + (-_LightPow);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat0.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat2.xxx;

    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;

    u_xlat2.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat2.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;

    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_1.x;

    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat6.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat6.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat3.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat3.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;

precision highp int;
uniform 	vec4 _DarkColor;
uniform 	vec4 _DownColor;
uniform 	vec4 _RimColor;
uniform 	float _HighBlend;
uniform 	float _HighOffset;
uniform 	float _HighColor;

uniform 	mediump float _Cutoff;
uniform 	mediump float _NormalStrong;
uniform 	mediump float _CustomAlpha;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _SSSColor;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _ExposureColor;
uniform lowp sampler2D _MainTex;
uniform lowp sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
uniform lowp sampler2D _RampMap;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
#define SV_Target0 gl_FragData[0]
vec3 u_xlat0;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
lowp vec3 u_xlat10_2;
bool u_xlatb2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
lowp vec3 u_xlat10_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_19;
float u_xlat20;
void main()
{
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat10_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat10_3.xyz = texture2D(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat10_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalStrong, _NormalStrong));
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-vs_TEXCOORD2.zxy) + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = inversesqrt(u_xlat20);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat20) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat3.yzx * (-vs_TEXCOORD2.zxy);
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.yzx) * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = inversesqrt(u_xlat20);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat20) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat10_2.xyz = texture2D(_RampMap, u_xlat16_1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat3.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat3.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat3.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat10_0.w * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat0.xyz = (-_DarkColor.xyz) + _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD3.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz + _DarkColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _SSSColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = _DownColor.xyz + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(vec3(_HighColor, _HighColor, _HighColor)) * u_xlat3.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + (-_DownColor.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD0.w + _HighOffset;
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat18 = log2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * _HighBlend;
    u_xlat18 = exp2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz + _DownColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD0.zzz * _RimColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD3.w * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat10_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat18) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_19) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz / u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    SV_Target0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    SV_Target0.w = _CustomAlpha;
    return;
}

{
    u_xlat0.x = (-_LightPow) + _LightOffset;
    u_xlat0.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat6.x = max(u_xlat6.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat6.x);
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat6.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat0.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat2.xxx;

    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;

    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat0.x) + 1.0;

    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;

{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalStrong, _NormalStrong));
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;

    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;

    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);

    u_xlat20 = inversesqrt(u_xlat20);

    u_xlat20 = inversesqrt(u_xlat20);

    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);

    u_xlat3.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;

    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_0.w * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat0.xyz = (-_DarkColor.xyz) + _SpecularColor.xyz;

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _SSSColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = _DownColor.xyz + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(vec3(_HighColor, _HighColor, _HighColor)) * u_xlat3.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + (-_DownColor.xyz);

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18 = log2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * _HighBlend;
    u_xlat18 = exp2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz + _DownColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD0.zzz * _RimColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD3.w * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat18) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_19) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz / u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);

    SV_Target0.w = _CustomAlpha;

    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * _HighBlend;
    u_xlat18 = exp2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz + _DownColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD0.zzz * _RimColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD3.w * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat10_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat18) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_19) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + (-unity_FogColor.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD11.www * u_xlat16_1.xyz + unity_FogColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz / u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    SV_Target0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    SV_Target0.w = _CustomAlpha;
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat6.x = max(u_xlat6.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat6.x);
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat6.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + (-_LightPow);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat2.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat0.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat2.xxx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat3.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat6.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = u_xlat2.z * u_xlat0.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.w = in_POSITION0.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * unity_LightmapST.xy + unity_LightmapST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_5.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_5.y;
    u_xlat16_1.w = u_xlat16_5.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_1;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat2.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat2.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_7 = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_1.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_7)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_1.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_1.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_1.z;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat6.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat6.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat3.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat3.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;

{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);

    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalStrong, _NormalStrong));
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-vs_TEXCOORD2.zxy) + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = inversesqrt(u_xlat20);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat20) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat3.yzx * (-vs_TEXCOORD2.zxy);
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.yzx) * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);

    u_xlat20 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = inversesqrt(u_xlat20);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat20) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_RampMap, u_xlat16_1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(unity_Lightmap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy).wxyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yzw * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat3.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat3.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat3.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat20) * u_xlat3.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_0.w * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat0.xyz = (-_DarkColor.xyz) + _SpecularColor.xyz;

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _SSSColor.xyz;

    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(vec3(_HighColor, _HighColor, _HighColor)) * u_xlat3.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + (-_DownColor.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD0.w + _HighOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18 = log2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * _HighBlend;
    u_xlat18 = exp2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz + _DownColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD0.zzz * _RimColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD3.w * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat18) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_19) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz / u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    SV_Target0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    SV_Target0.w = _CustomAlpha;
    return;
}

    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat6.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat6.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat3.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat3.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat0.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat2.xxxx;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0 = min(max(u_xlat0, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0 = clamp(u_xlat0, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = u_xlat0;
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 300 es

precision highp float;
precision highp int;
#define HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS 1
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
#define UNITY_UNIFORM
#else
#define UNITY_UNIFORM uniform
#endif
#define UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION 1
#if UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x) layout(location = x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(binding = x, std140)
#else
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(std140)
#endif
uniform 	vec4 _DarkColor;
uniform 	vec4 _DownColor;
uniform 	vec4 _RimColor;
uniform 	float _HighBlend;
uniform 	float _HighOffset;
uniform 	float _HighColor;
uniform 	float _MaxShadow;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[4];
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_FogColor;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _GIDiffuseColor;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _ExposureColor;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(0) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _UVScallePaner;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cutoff;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _NormalStrong;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RenderType;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cull;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ZWrite;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ZTest;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AlphaToMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SrcBlendFactor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DstBlendFactor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SrcBlendFactorAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DstBlendFactorAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _BlendOp;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _BlendOpAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _CustomAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _Frequency;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _Amplitude;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _WaveLength;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Power;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SSSColor;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D unity_Lightmap;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
bool u_xlatb2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_19;
float u_xlat20;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalStrong, _NormalStrong));
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-vs_TEXCOORD2.zxy) + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = inversesqrt(u_xlat20);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat20) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat3.yzx * (-vs_TEXCOORD2.zxy);
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.yzx) * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat20 = inversesqrt(u_xlat20);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat20) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_RampMap, u_xlat16_1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(unity_Lightmap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy).wxyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yzw * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);
    u_xlat20 = max(u_xlat16_3.x, _MaxShadow);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat3.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat3.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat3.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat20) * u_xlat3.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_0.w * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat0.xyz = (-_DarkColor.xyz) + _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD3.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz + _DarkColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _SSSColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = _DownColor.xyz + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(vec3(_HighColor, _HighColor, _HighColor)) * u_xlat3.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + (-_DownColor.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD0.w + _HighOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18 = log2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * _HighBlend;
    u_xlat18 = exp2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz + _DownColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD0.zzz * _RimColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = vs_TEXCOORD3.w * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat18) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_19) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + (-unity_FogColor.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD11.www * u_xlat16_1.xyz + unity_FogColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz / u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    SV_Target0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    SV_Target0.w = _CustomAlpha;
    return;
}

#endif
"
}

"// hash: 7e1f6e5f7ab0171f
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 100

uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowBias;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
uniform 	vec3 _LightDirection;
attribute highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position.z = max((-u_xlat0.w), u_xlat0.z);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

#endif

    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;

    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat6 = min(max(u_xlat6, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position.z = max((-u_xlat0.w), u_xlat0.z);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}
